## Ethereum Improvement Proposals

* Ethereum Improvement Proposals

- [ ethereum/EIPs](https://github.com/ethereum/EIPs)

Ethereum Improvement Proposals (EIPs) describe standards for the Ethereum platform, such as core protocol specifications.
